    SELECT [i].[Id], [i].[CreatedDate], [i].[JogoId], [i].[PedidoId], [i].[PrecoUnitario], [i].[Quantidade], [j].[Id] AS [Id0], [j].[CreatedDate] AS [CreatedDate0], [j].[IsPromotional], [j].[Preco], [j].[Titulo]
    FROM [ItemPedido] AS [i]
    INNER JOIN [Jogo] AS [j] ON [i].[JogoId] = [j].[Id]
) AS [t1] ON [t0].[Id] = [t1].[PedidoId]
ORDER BY [t0].[Id], [t0].[Id0], [t1].[Id]
